            <p>When there is a significant difference in electronegativity between the O atom and the TM atom, the TM─O bond will express more ionic properties, as shown in Figure&nbsp;<a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0006">6h</a>. The electron cloud around the O atom and the TM atom is close to and overlaps. Due to the significant difference in electronegativity between the two atoms, the electron cloud will polarize and shift toward the O atom, which can also be understood as the O atom gaining electrons, the TM atom losing electrons, and the O ion and TM ion forming ionic molecular bonds through electrostatic interaction, in this case, the O atom no longer retains the non-bonded electrons of O 2<i>p</i>.</p>
            
            <p>The ELF calculation results indicate that when the electronegativity of the three TM atoms bonded to the O atom is similar, the TM-O molecular bond does not exhibit significant covalent or ionic properties, and there are no non-bonded electrons of O 2<i>p</i>. When the electronegativity of three TM atoms is two large and one small, the two TM─O bonds exhibit partial covalence. The electrons of the O atom form two sets of covalent bonds with the two TM atoms, and the probability of remaining non-bonded electrons of O 2<i>p</i> is extremely low. When the electronegativity of three TM atoms is two small and one large, there is a probability of retaining O 2<i>p</i> non-bonded electrons. So only in the electronegativity-difference configuration of Fe-O-Mn<sub>2</sub> and Ni-O-Mn<sub>2</sub> (electronegativity: Mn = 1.55, Fe = 1.83, Ni = 1.91), there will be lO<sub>2</sub><i><sub>p</sub></i> lone pair electrons, exhibiting reversible redox properties of oxygen ions.</p>
            
            <p>Interestingly, the ELF calculation results indicate that when La<sup>3+</sup> occupies the TM position of Fe<sup>3+</sup>, forming La-O-TM<sub>2</sub> configuration, quasi-non-bonded O 2<i>p</i> states will be generated in the direction of La─O bond, which indicates that La doping can effectively enhance the activity of oxygen participation in the reaction, as shown in Figure&nbsp;<a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0006">6b</a>. The electronegativity of La is relatively small at 1.11, and the La─O bond exhibits more ionic bond properties as shown in Figure&nbsp;<a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0006">6i</a>. The extranuclear electronic structure of La<sup>3+</sup> is [Xe], with all 4<i>f</i> orbitals empty and all 5<i>p</i> orbitals full. At this point, La<sup>3+</sup> exhibits hard ion properties. The special arrangement of extranuclear electrons makes it difficult for the La electron cloud to be disturbed by the O electron cloud, so the interaction between the two electron clouds is limited. In this case, a portion of O electrons will not participate in the formation of ionic bonds, thus retaining the non-bonded electrons of O 2<i>p</i> orbitals with a certain probability. Therefore, regardless of the electronegativity configuration, as long as La atoms participate in bonding, there will be non-bonded electrons of O 2<i>p</i> orbitals. This is the mechanism by which La<sup>3+</sup> activates the redox reaction of oxygen. Some other works also showed that M ions doping which have <i>d</i>-electron-empty orbitals could make a great improvement in electrochemical performance.<sup>[</sup><span><sup><a href="#adfm202404797-bib-0007" class="bibLink tab-link" id="adfm202404797-bib-0007_R_d261997663e2127" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 7 - Adv. Energy Mater. Energy Environ. Sci. Joule Joule J. Mater. Chem. A Joule Adv. Energy Mater. Adv. Energy Mater. Chem. Mater. Chem. Mater. Electrochem. Commun. Energy Environ. Sci. J. Mater. Sci. Technol. Nat. Sustain.">7</a>, <a href="#adfm202404797-bib-0029" class="bibLink tab-link" id="adfm202404797-bib-0029_R_d261997663e2127" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 29 - Adv. Funct. Mater. J. Phys. Chem. C">29</a></sup></span><sup>]</sup></p>
            
            <p>ELF iso-surface for medium value (0.046&nbsp;eV) of MFN and La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN are shown in Figure&nbsp;<a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0006">6c,d</a>, respectively. A local basin shared between two atoms at medium ELF value indicates the occurrence of covalent bonds between these two atoms. While Ni─O bond is clearly covalent, Mn─O bond and La─O bond appear mainly ionic, because there will be varying degrees of localized electrons on the surfaces of La, Mn, and Fe.</p>
            
            <p>The calculation results of partial density of states (pDOS) of MFN and La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN are shown in Figure&nbsp;<a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0006">6e,f</a>, respectively. The red shaded area is O 2<i>p</i> in non-bonded state. In the modified sample, this area increases, which is consistent with ELF calculation results. The results show that La doping will enhance the redox activity of oxygen.</p>
            
            <p>To reveal the result of reversible anionic redox, the pDOS be calculated for both MFN and 2%-La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN charged to 4.3&nbsp;V and discharged to 3.75&nbsp;V, respectively. The results are shown in Figure <a class="suppLink scrollableLink" href="#support-information-section">S15</a> (Supporting Information).</p>
            
            <p>To calculate the number of transferred electrons, integration is performed on O<sub>2p</sub>. In the initial state, the pDOS of O<sub>2</sub><i><sub>p</sub></i> area ratios below the Fermi level in MFN and 2%-La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN are both 86%. When charged to 4.3&nbsp;V, the area ratios below the Fermi level in MFN and 2%-La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN are 71% and 70%, respectively. This means that 15% and 16% of electrons transferred. When discharged to 3.75&nbsp;V, the area ratios below the Fermi level in MFN and 2%-La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN are 74% and 76% respectively. This indicates that only 3% and 6% of electrons transfer are reversible, which is consistent with the conclusion obtained from initial galvanostatic charge/discharge profiles at 0.05 C. The pDOS results show that there are more electrons can be removed from lO<sub>2</sub><i><sub>p</sub></i> in modified material, and the anion redox in modified material is more reversible.</p>
            
            <p>After coating La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>, the rate performance of the material is improved, mainly because the lattice structure is changed after La<sup>3+</sup> diffuse into the lattice. After modification, Na layer becomes wider (3.6464 vs 3.6252 Å), and Na-O becomes longer (2.3615 Å vs 2.3557 Å). Wider Na layer can ensure that Na ions can migrate more smoothly, and the increased Na─O bond length decreases the Coulomb force between Na<sup>+</sup> and O<sup>2−</sup>, and the potential barrier of migration is reduced, which is favorable to the migration of Na<sup>+</sup>. To prove the above point, the bond valence energy landscape (BVEL) and electron density maps (EDM) calculations were carried out. <b>Figure</b> <a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0007">7a,b</a> show the Na<sup>+</sup> diffusion channels of MFN and La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN, respectively. The BVEL results show that the minimum permeability energy of material La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN is 1.25&nbsp;eV, which is less than that of the bare sample (1.32&nbsp;eV). At the same 1.25&nbsp;eV energy condition, the Na<sup>+</sup> diffusion channel of the bare sample is significantly narrower than that of the modified sample. Figure&nbsp;<a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0007">7c,d</a> shows the EDM calculation results of MFN and La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN, respectively, the iso-surface value is 0.6&nbsp;eV. The results show that at the same energy (0.6&nbsp;eV), the electron cloud of Na atom and O atom of sample MFN overlaps more closely (dashed circle area), so the Coulomb force of Na<sup>+</sup> and O<sup>2−</sup> is stronger and Na<sup>+</sup> is not easy to diffuse.</p>
            
            <section class="article-section__inline-figure">
               <figure class="figure" id="adfm202404797-fig-0007"><a target="_blank" href="/cms/asset/290e1ca1-5c14-4855-ba21-a00772a62508/adfm202404797-fig-0007-m.jpg"><picture>
                        <source srcset="/cms/asset/290e1ca1-5c14-4855-ba21-a00772a62508/adfm202404797-fig-0007-m.jpg" media="(min-width: 1650px)"><img class="figure__image" src="/cms/asset/d09a5d05-74eb-466a-a2d6-2f7be477de63/adfm202404797-fig-0007-m.png" data-lg-src="/cms/asset/290e1ca1-5c14-4855-ba21-a00772a62508/adfm202404797-fig-0007-m.jpg" alt="Details are in the caption following the image" title="Details are in the caption following the image" loading="lazy"></picture></a><figcaption class="figure__caption">
                     <div class="figure__caption__header"><strong class="figure__title">Figure 7<span style="font-weight:normal"></span></strong><div class="figure-extra"><a href="#" class="open-figure-link">Open in figure viewer</a><a href="/action/downloadFigures?id=adfm202404797-fig-0007&amp;partId=&amp;doi=10.1002%2Fadfm.202404797" class="ppt-figure-link"><i aria-hidden="true" class="icon-Icon_Download"></i><span>PowerPoint</span></a></div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="figure__caption figure__caption-text">The results of BVEL calculation for a) MFN and b) 2%-La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN. The results of EDM calculation for c) MFN and d) 2%-La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN, the iso-surface value is 0.6&nbsp;eV. The results of EDM calculation for e) MFN and f) 2%-La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN, the iso-surface value is 0.3&nbsp;eV.</div>
                  </figcaption>
               </figure>
            </section>
            <p>After modification, the lattice structure of the material has changed. TM layer becomes narrower (1.7836 vs 1.7951 Å), which can ensure that the material skeleton is more stable. TM─O bond length becomes shorter (2.0166 vs 2.0236 Å), and the reduced TM─O bond length increases the Coulomb force between TM ions and O<sup>2−</sup>, which increases the lattice energy and thus enhances the lattice stability. Figure&nbsp;<a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0007">7e,f</a> shows the EDM calculation results of MFN and La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN, respectively, the iso-surface value is 0.3&nbsp;eV. The results show that at the same energy (0.3&nbsp;eV), the electron cloud of TM atom and O atom of La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN overlaps more closely (dashed circle area), so the Coulomb force of TM ions and O<sup>2−</sup> is stronger and the structure is more stable. In addition, the calculation results of BVEL show that in the bare sample, the minimum permeation energies of Mn, Fe and Ni atoms in the <i>a</i> and <i>b</i> directions are 3.13, 1.52, and 1.41&nbsp;eV, respectively, and in the modified sample are 3.26, 1.61, and 1.48&nbsp;eV, respectively. The calculation results show that La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN has stronger structural strength. At the same time, La<sup>3+</sup> doping into the lattice can enhance the stability and reversibility of OAR, to improve the long cycle stability of the material. Under high voltage, O<sup>2−</sup> will undergo redox reaction and lose electrons. Because of the loss of electrons, two adjacent oxygen will be close to each other to form O─O dimer. O─O dimer, due to its oxidizing nature, can react with the electrolyte, causing oxygen loss and irreversible structure, which is one of the important reasons for the poor long cycle performance of materials. The calculation results show that La doping increases the Coulomb force between O atoms and makes it difficult to form O─O dimer and easy to restore the O─O bond structure. The EDM calculation results are shown in Figure&nbsp;<a href="#adfm202404797-fig-0007">7c,d</a> (dashed circle Areas 1 and 2).</p>
            </section>
         </section>
      <section class="article-section__content" id="adfm202404797-sec-0080">
         
         <h2 class="article-section__title section__title section1" id="adfm202404797-sec-0080-title">3 Conclusion</h2>
         
         <p>In a summary, we found that in O3-type cathode NaMn<sub>1/3</sub>Fe<sub>1/3</sub>Ni<sub>1/3</sub>O<sub>2</sub>, the electronegativity-difference configuration plays a key role on the activation of the reversible OAR and we further propose to tune electronegativity-difference configuration with La<sup>3+</sup> doping to construct lO<sub>2</sub><i><sub>p</sub></i> orbitals for reversible anionic redox in O3-type cathode. The research results indicate that, in the octahedral configuration, when the electronegativity configuration of the three TM atoms bonded to O is two weak and one strong, there will be non-bonded electrons of O 2<i>p</i>, thereby trigger reversible OAR. By doping with La<sup>3+</sup> and utilizing the special extranuclear electronic structure of La<sup>3+</sup> [Xe], the La electron cloud is difficult to be disturbed by the O electron cloud, and some O electrons will not participate in the formation of ionic bonds, thus retaining the non-bonded electrons of O 2<i>p</i> and activating OAR. In addition, La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub> coating layer hinders the direct contact of the material with the electrolyte, thereby inhibiting the reaction between molecular oxygen and the electrolyte, making OAR reversible. La<sup>3+</sup> doping regulates the lattice structure, and the decreased Coulomb force between Na<sup>+</sup> and O<sup>2−</sup> favors Na<sup>+</sup> migration. The increased Coulomb force between TM ion and O<sup>2−</sup> and the strong La─O bonds inhibit the irreversible phase transition and stabilize the structure. After modification, 2%-La<sub>2</sub>O<sub>3</sub>@MFN material shows excellent high capacity and long cycle stability whose capacity retention rate remains above 90% after 300 cycles at 5 C. This study has a guiding significance for realizing high capacity, high rate and long cycle retention by regulating OAR in SIBs.</p>
         </section>
      <div class="article-section__content">

                  <div tabindex="0" class="section__title" id="support-information-section"><span>Supporting Information</span><i aria-hidden="true" class="icon-section_arrow_d"></i></div></a></h2>
            <div class="accordion__content" role="region" aria-labelledby="support-information-section" style="display: none;" id="adfm202404797-supinfo-0001" aria-hidden="false">
